    prettyPrintJson = function(temp_761)
        local str11 = "  ";
        local value29 = 0;
        local str12 = "";
        local value30 = 1;
        local value31 = false;
        while value30 <= #temp_761 do
            local var252 = temp_761:sub(value30, value30);
            if var252 == "\"" and temp_761:sub(value30 - 1, value30 - 1) ~= "\\" then
                value31 = not value31;
                str12 = str12 .. var252;
            else
                if value31 then
                    str12 = str12 .. var252;
                else
                    if var252 == "{" or var252 == "[" then
                        str12 = str12 .. var252 .. "\n" .. str11:rep(value29 + 1);
                        value29 = value29 + 1;
                    else
                        if var252 == "}" or var252 == "]" then
                            value29 = value29 - 1;
                            str12 = str12 .. "\n" .. str11:rep(value29) .. var252;
                        else
                            if var252 == "," then
                                str12 = str12 .. var252 .. "\n" .. str11:rep(value29);
                            else
                                if var252 == ":" then
                                    str12 = str12 .. var252 .. " ";
                                else
                                    if not var252:match("%s") then
                                        str12 = str12 .. var252;
                                    end;
                                end;
                            end;
                        end;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
            value30 = value30 + 1;
        end;
        return str12;
    end;

            end;

        end);
    end;
